{\bfseries Value\-:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
(pSYTM)->tm\_hour = (pSYSTIME)->wHour;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_min  = (pSYSTIME)->wMinute;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_sec  = (pSYSTIME)->wSecond;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_mon  = (pSYSTIME)->wMonth - 1;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_mday = (pSYSTIME)->wDay;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_year = (pSYSTIME)->wYear;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_yday = 0;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_wday = (pSYSTIME)->wDayOfWeek;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_gmtoff = 0;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_isdst = -1;\(\backslash\)
         (pSYTM)->tm\_zone = 0;
